msg:Crowne Plaza Guangzhou Zengcheng: Enjoy the beautiful river views as you wish

I have stayed in this hotel too many times, and every time I upgraded to a suite. This time, because of the shortage of rooms due to large conferences, I was not upgraded to a suite for the first time. The river view is so beautiful. After a tiring day, looking at the river from a room on a high floor, infinite sadness instantly turns into infinite joy. Manager Ye on duty was very polite and left a deep impression.‚Äã‚Äã

The breakfast room on the first floor has private rooms and a members-only area. It is similar to the executive lounge. It is based on the European palace style and is decorated with Chinese style elements, such as classical vases. The most amazing dish in the breakfast and executive lounge is the pork neck, which is fat but not greasy, chewy and refreshing, and you will never get tired of eating it. The pork neck in the breakfast room is fried raw, which has a more original taste; the pork neck in the lounge is fried, which makes you feel happy. The gym is not 24 hours a day because it has been outsourced. There are many students who come here for yoga classes, fitness classes and swimming classes. I recall that three years ago when the epidemic hit, I came to stay in this hotel. The gym was already empty and lifeless. Now it is full of life again, which is gratifying.‚Äã‚Äã

The staff training in the executive lounge is quite inadequate. Whether it is cleaning, chefs or reception staff, they completely ignore the guests. Even if a group of guests are dining, they are just chatting among themselves. When receiving the meal, they loudly comment on various dishes, and then Everyone "cleans" their favorite leftovers, which really makes people stunned. The lounge is on the top floor, with beautiful scenery, high ceilings, exquisite decoration, and a wide variety of dishes, desserts, drinks, and drinks. Every time I go to the China Eastern Airlines or China Southern Airlines lounge at Baiyun Airport, the staff will give me butterfly cakes as souvenirs, but compared with the desserts from Zengcheng Poly CP, there is still a gap.‚Äã‚Äã

Hong Kong's "Yuen Long Wing Wah" now has only one store in Guangzhou (there used to be two), which is just downstairs from Shifu VOCO. Every time I buy a lot of wife cakes there and then take them to the exhibition hall the next day and share them with the models, makeup artists, hostesses, and staff backstage. They are actually the ones who have made the most obscure efforts. By. The route I usually take is: after leaving the exhibition hall, take the subway to Xingang East Station, take 13 stops to Hualin Temple Station, go out to buy cakes, then get off from Exit E of Hualin Temple Station, and take the subway for one hour and 19 minutes. Go to Xintang Station, exit from Exit D2 and take a taxi. You can reach Zengcheng CP within about five kilometers.
